The minimalist interface hides a number of powerful writing features\r\n\r\nWORDCOUNT TOOLS\r\n===============\r\nSee at a glance how many words are in your document, or how many you've written since you opened the app. \r\n\r\nWORDCOUNT GOAL\r\n==============\r\nSet yourself a target - for example, 500 words - and Poe will let you know when you've reached that goal with a non-intrusive toast notification\r\n\r\nWRITING TIMER\r\n=============\r\nGot a limited amount of time to write? Set yourself an alarm to let you know when it's time to stop writing. Writers know it's all too easy to get caught up in the story and lose track of time. \r\n\r\nAUTOSAVE \r\n========\r\nImproved autosave features mean you never lose work. Poe saves right back to the file you opened. It also keeps any unsaved work in temp files. If you close the app and forget to save, Poe resurrects your work and prompts you to save it this time. This also protects against unexpected events like powercuts, battery rundown, windows 8 suspending the app in the background or even a system crash. You can now also change how often poe autosaves. \r\n\r\nCUSTOM THEMES\r\n=============\r\nPoe comes with three preset themes: Dark, Grey, and Light. Don't like them? No problem.
